<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Language_tools">Language tools</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Latin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: Language tools">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1"><a class="external text" href="https://www.perseus.tufts.edu/hopper/resolveform?lang=la" rel="nofollow">"Latin Dictionary Headword Search"</a>. <i>Perseus Hopper</i>. Tufts University.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.jtitle=Perseus+Hopper&amp;rft.atitle=Latin+Dictionary+Headword+Search&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.perseus.tufts.edu%2Fhopper%2Fresolveform%3Flang%3Dla&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALatin"></span> Searches Lewis &amp; Short's <i>A Latin Dictionary</i> and Lewis's <i>An Elementary Latin Dictionary</i>. Online results.</li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1"><a class="external text" href="https://www.online-latin-dictionary.com" rel="nofollow">"Online Latin Dictionary with conjugator and declension tool"</a>. Olivetti Media Communication.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Online+Latin+Dictionary+with+conjugator+and+declension+tool&amp;rft.pub=Olivetti+Media+Communication&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.online-latin-dictionary.com&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALatin"></span> Search on line Latin-English and English-Latin dictionary with complete declension or conjugation. Online results.</li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1"><a class="external text" href="https://www.perseus.tufts.edu/hopper/morph?lang=la" rel="nofollow">"Latin Word Study Tool"</a>. <i>Perseus Hopper</i>. Tufts University.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.jtitle=Perseus+Hopper&amp;rft.atitle=Latin+Word+Study+Tool&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.perseus.tufts.edu%2Fhopper%2Fmorph%3Flang%3Dla&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALatin"></span> Identifies the grammatical functions of words entered. Online results.</li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1" id="CITEREFAversa">Aversa, Alan. <a class="external text" href="https://www.u.arizona.edu/~aversa/latin/" rel="nofollow">"Latin Inflector"</a>. University of Arizona.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Latin+Inflector&amp;rft.pub=University+of+Arizona&amp;rft.aulast=Aversa&amp;rft.aufirst=Alan&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.u.arizona.edu%2F~aversa%2Flatin%2F&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALatin"></span> Identifies the grammatical functions of all the words in sentences entered, using Perseus.</li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1"><a class="external text" href="https://www.verbix.com/languages/latin.shtml" rel="nofollow">"Latin Verb Conjugator"</a>. Verbix.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Latin+Verb+Conjugator&amp;rft.pub=Verbix&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.verbix.com%2Flanguages%2Flatin.shtml&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALatin"></span> Displays complete conjugations of verbs entered in first-person present singular form.</li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1"><a class="external text" href="http://arquivo.pt/wayback/20160518085747/https://stranica.net63.net/verba_latina" rel="nofollow">"Online Latin Verb Conjugator"</a>. Archived from <a class="external text" href="https://stranica.net63.net/verba_latina" rel="nofollow">the original</a> on 18 May 2016<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">30 September</span> 2014</span>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Online+Latin+Verb+Conjugator&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fstranica.net63.net%2Fverba_latina&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALatin"></span> Displays conjugation of verbs entered in their infinitive form.</li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1" id="CITEREFWhittaker">Whittaker, William. <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20060618211448/https://lysy2.archives.nd.edu/cgi-bin/words.exe" rel="nofollow">"Words"</a>. Notre Dame Archives. Archived from <a class="external text" href="https://lysy2.archives.nd.edu/cgi-bin/words.exe" rel="nofollow">the original</a> on 18 June 2006.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Words&amp;rft.pub=Notre+Dame+Archives&amp;rft.aulast=Whittaker&amp;rft.aufirst=William&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Flysy2.archives.nd.edu%2Fcgi-bin%2Fwords.exe&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALatin"></span> Identifies Latin words entered. Translates English words entered.</li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1"><a class="external text" href="https://alpheios.net" rel="nofollow">"Alpheios"</a>. Alpheios Project.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Alpheios&amp;rft.pub=Alpheios+Project&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Falpheios.net&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALatin"></span> Combines Whittakers Words, Lewis and Short, Bennett's grammar and inflection tables in a browser addon.</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://curlie.org/Reference/Dictionaries/World_Languages/L/Latin/" rel="nofollow">Latin Dictionaries</a> at <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Curlie" title="Curlie">Curlie</a></li>
<li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation book cs1" id="CITEREFDymock1830">Dymock, John (1830). <a class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=2sIDAAAAQAAJ" rel="nofollow"><i>A new abridgment of Ainsworth's Dictionary, English and Latin, for the use of Grammar Schools</i></a> (4th ed.). Glasgow: Hutchison &amp; Brookman.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=book&amp;rft.btitle=A+new+abridgment+of+Ainsworth%27s+Dictionary%2C+English+and+Latin%2C+for+the+use+of+Grammar+Schools&amp;rft.place=Glasgow&amp;rft.edition=4th&amp;rft.pub=Hutchison+%26+Brookman&amp;rft.date=1830&amp;rft.aulast=Dymock&amp;rft.aufirst=John&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fbooks.google.com%2Fbooks%3Fid%3D2sIDAAAAQAAJ&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALatin"></span></li>
<li>"<a class="external text" href="https://docs.cltk.org/en/latest/latin.html" rel="nofollow">Classical Language Toolkit</a> <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20160524154553/https://docs.cltk.org/en/latest/latin.html" rel="nofollow">Archived</a> 24 May 2016 at the <a href="/wiki/Wayback_Machine" title="Wayback Machine">Wayback Machine</a>" (CLTK). A <a href="/wiki/Natural_language_processing" title="Natural language processing">Natural language processing</a> toolkit for <a href="/wiki/Python_(programming_language)" title="Python (programming language)">Python</a> offering a variety of functionality for Latin and other classical languages.</li>
<li>"<a class="external text" href="https://outils.biblissima.fr/en/collatinus-web/index.php" rel="nofollow">Collatinus web</a>". Online lemmatizer and morphological analysis for Latin texts.</li></ul>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Phonetics">Phonetics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Latin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=46" title="Edit section: Phonetics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><link href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1067248974" rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style"/><cite class="citation web cs1" id="CITEREFCui2005">Cui, Ray (2005). <a class="external text" href="https://la.raycui.com/" rel="nofollow">"Phonetica Latinae-How to pronounce Latin"</a>. Ray Cui<span class="reference-accessdate">. Retrieved <span class="nowrap">25 June</span> 2010</span>.</cite><span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Phonetica+Latinae-How+to+pronounce+Latin&amp;rft.pub=Ray+Cui&amp;rft.date=2005&amp;rft.aulast=Cui&amp;rft.aufirst=Ray&amp;rft_id=https%3A%2F%2Fla.raycui.com%2F&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3ALatin"></span></li>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Libraries">Libraries</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Latin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Libraries">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a class="external text" href="https://www.thelatinlibrary.com/" rel="nofollow">The latin library</a>, ancient Latin books and writings (without translations) ordered by author</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://penelope.uchicago.edu/Thayer/E/Roman/Texts/" rel="nofollow">LacusCurtius</a>, a small collection of Greek and Roman authors along with their books and writings (original texts are in Latin and Greek, translations in English and occasionally in a few other languages are available)</li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Latin_language_news_and_audio">Latin language news and audio</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Latin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Latin language news and audio">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><a class="external text" href="https://ephemeris.alcuinus.net/" rel="nofollow">Ephemeris</a>, online Latin newspaper: <span title="Latin-language text"><i lang="la">nuntii latini universi</i></span> = news in Latin of the universe (whole world)</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20190830212232/https://ephemeris.alcuinus.net/" rel="nofollow">Ephemeris archive</a>, archived copy of online Latin newspaper</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://yle.fi/radio1/tiede/nuntii_latini/" rel="nofollow">Nuntii Latini</a>, from Finnish YLE Radio 1</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://www.bremenzwei.de/themen/nuntii-latini-100.html" rel="nofollow">Nuntii Latini</a>, monthly review from German <a href="/wiki/Radio_Bremen" title="Radio Bremen">Radio Bremen</a> (<a href="/wiki/Bremen_Zwei" title="Bremen Zwei">Bremen Zwei</a>)</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20150129091342/https://www.haverford.edu/classics/audio/" rel="nofollow">Classics Podcasts in Latin and Ancient Greek</a>, Haverford College</li>
<li><a class="external text" href="https://sites.google.com/site/janualinguae/latin" rel="nofollow">Latinum Latin Language course and Latin Language YouTube Index</a></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Latin_language_online_communities">Latin language online communities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Latin&amp;action=edit&amp;section=49" title="Edit section: Latin language online communities">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3 class="vector-menu-heading" id="p-personal-label">
<span class="vector-menu-heading-label">Personal tools</span>
